  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "DOI:10.1186/s12885-022-09872-y" 

- [M0 macrophage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020017) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A macrophage that has not yet undergone polarization into a specific macrophage subtype. These cells are non-activated and have the potential to differentiate into inflammatory (M1) or alternatively activated (M2) macrophage subtypes in response to appropriate stimuli." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:30861466" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "DOI:10.1186/s12885-022-09872-y"

### alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-sustained (Mmus) `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020024`

#### Added

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-sustained (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020024) [present in taxon](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002175) [Mus musculus](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/NCBITaxon_10090) 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-sustained (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020024) [contributor](http://purl.org/dc/terms/contributor) [0000-0002-5507-2103](https://orcid.org/0000-0002-5507-2103) 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-sustained (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020024) [creator](http://purl.org/dc/terms/creator) "GitHub Copilot" 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-sustained (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020024) [in_subset](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#inSubset) [mouse_subset](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/cl#mouse_subset) 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-sustained (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020024) [has exact synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "G5" 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:26735013" 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-sustained (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020024) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A mouse retinal ganglion cell type defined by a large soma and a wide, monostratified dendritic arbor that stratifies just distal to the outer ChAT band of the inner plexiform layer (Krieger et al., 2017). It corresponds to the G5 physiological type (Baden et al., 2016; Goetz et al., 2022) and the C42 transcriptomic cluster (Tran et al., 2019), and is considered the evolutionary ortholog of the primate OFF midget RGC (Hahn et al., 2023). The cell projects a thick, fast-conducting axon to the dorsal lateral geniculate nucleus and superior colliculus. It shows a sustained increase in firing to light decrements with a slow decay time constant of roughly 250 ms and a large receptive field center with weak surround antagonism (Krieger et al., 2017). Its molecular profile includes expression of Spp1 and Neurofilament (Smi32) together with Brn3a (Pou4f1) and Brn3b (Pou4f2), absence of Brn3c (Pou4f3) and Calbindin (Calb1), and strong enrichment of Fes (Krieger et al., 2017; Tran et al., 2019)." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:35830791" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:28753612" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:26735013" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:37066415" 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-sustained (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020024) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "The G-type nomenclature used here refers specifically to the functional classification of mouse retinal ganglion cells introduced by Baden and colleagues, and is distinct from earlier G-based schemes used for rabbit or other species. Readers should be aware that the same letter&ndash;number labels (e.g., &quot;G1&quot;, &quot;G2&quot;) have been applied in different historical contexts to different animals and criteria (functional vs. morphological), so cross-species or cross-era comparisons of &quot;G&quot; names should not be assumed equivalent without explicit mapping in the primary literature." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:26735013" 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-sustained (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020024) [has_related_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasRelatedSynonym) "alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-s" 
  - [has_synonym_type](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasSynonymType) [abbreviation](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/OMO_0003000) 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:28753612" 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-sustained (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020024) [has exact synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "C42" 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:31784286"

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-transient (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020026) [term tracker item](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000233) "https://github.com/obophenotype/cell-ontology/issues/3493" 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-transient (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020026) [contributor](http://purl.org/dc/terms/contributor) [0000-0002-5507-2103](https://orcid.org/0000-0002-5507-2103) 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-transient (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020026) [creator](http://purl.org/dc/terms/creator) "GitHub Copilot" 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-transient (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020026) [creation_date](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#creation_date) "2025-12-05T11:29:19Z"^^[dateTime](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#dateTime) 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-transient (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020026) [in_subset](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#inSubset) [mouse_subset](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/cl#mouse_subset) 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-transient (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020026) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "An alpha retinal ganglion cell subtype found in the mouse retina that responds selectively and transiently to decreases in light intensity. It is characterized by a large soma, a broad dendritic arbor that stratifies within sublamina a of the inner plexiform layer, and rapid OFF-transient firing kinetics that decay even during sustained stimulation (Krieger et al., 2017). Functionally, it corresponds to G8 in the Baden functional classification (Baden et al., 2016; Goetz et al., 2022) and C45 in the Tran transcriptomic atlas (Tran et al., 2019), and it is considered the evolutionary ortholog of the primate OFF Parasol RGC (Hahn et al., 2023). This cell type acts as a detector of rapidly approaching dark objects and contributes to innate defensive responses by encoding looming stimuli (M&uuml;nch et al., 2009). It exhibits a distinctive molecular signature by its expression of Brn3c (Krieger et al., 2017)." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:35830791" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:28753612" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:26735013" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:37066415" 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-transient (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020026) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "The G-type nomenclature used here refers specifically to the functional classification of mouse retinal ganglion cells introduced by Baden and colleagues, and is distinct from earlier G-based schemes used for rabbit or other species. Readers should be aware that the same letter&ndash;number labels (e.g., &quot;G1&quot;, &quot;G2&quot;) have been applied in different historical contexts to different animals and criteria (functional vs. morphological), so cross-species or cross-era comparisons of &quot;G&quot; names should not be assumed equivalent without explicit mapping in the primary literature." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:26735013" 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-transient (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020026) [has_related_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasRelatedSynonym) "alpha retinal ganglion cell OFF-t" 
  - [has_synonym_type](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasSynonymType) [abbreviation](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/OMO_0003000) 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:28753612"

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell ON-sustained (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020025) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A retinal ganglion cell type that has a large soma and a wide, monostratified dendritic arbor that stratifies in the inner sublamina of the inner plexiform layer, with dendrites located just proximal to the inner ChAT band (Krieger et al., 2017). It shows a sustained increase in firing rate to ON stimuli (Krieger et al., 2017). It corresponds to the G24 functional type (Baden et al., 2016; Goetz et al., 2022), the C43 transcriptomic cluster (Tran et al., 2019), and is considered the mouse ortholog of the primate ON midget retinal ganglion cell (Hahn et al., 2023). It is molecularly defined by expression of Spp1, Smi32, Brn3b, Calbindin, and Tbr2 (Krieger et al., 2017; Tran et al., 2019)." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:35830791"

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell ON-transient (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020027) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "An alpha retinal ganglion cell subtype in the mouse retina that responds selectively and transiently to increases in light intensity. It possesses the large soma and expansive dendritic field characteristic of alpha RGCs (Krieger et al., 2017). This cell exhibits a brief, fast-decaying burst of firing at the onset of light increments and contributes to motion detection for luminance increases, forming the ON-branch of the transient magnocellular-like pathway (Krieger et al., 2017; Hahn et al., 2023). Functionally, it corresponds to cluster G19 and aligns transcriptomically with cluster C41 (Krieger et al., 2017; Tran et al., 2019). It is orthologous to the primate ON Parasol RGC (Hahn et al., 2023). Molecularly, it expresses Spp1, Smi32, and Brn3b, but lacks Brn3a, Brn3c, and Calbindin (Krieger et al., 2017)." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:35830791" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:31784286" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:28753612" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:26735013" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:37066415" 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell ON-transient (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020027) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "The G-type nomenclature used here refers specifically to the functional classification of mouse retinal ganglion cells introduced by Baden and colleagues, and is distinct from earlier G-based schemes used for rabbit or other species. Readers should be aware that the same letter&ndash;number labels (e.g., &quot;G1&quot;, &quot;G2&quot;) have been applied in different historical contexts to different animals and criteria (functional vs. morphological), so cross-species or cross-era comparisons of &quot;G&quot; names should not be assumed equivalent without explicit mapping in the primary literature." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:26735013" 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell ON-transient (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020027) [has_related_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasRelatedSynonym) "alpha retinal ganglion cell ON-t" 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:28753612" 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell ON-transient (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020027) [has exact synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "C41" 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:31784286" 

- [alpha retinal ganglion cell ON-transient (Mmus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020027) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "alpha retinal ganglion cell ON-transient (Mmus)"

#### Added
- [direct pathway medium spiny neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023026) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A GABAergic medium spiny neuron located in the striatum that gives rise to the direct basal ganglia pathway. It projects directly to the GPi and SNr, where it inhibits tonically active GABAergic output neurons to disinhibit thalamic and brainstem motor targets (Gerfen. 2023). In mice and humans, this cell selectively expresses the D1 dopamine receptor (DRD1), which couples to stimulatory G-proteins (Gs/G&alpha;olf) to increase cAMP and activate PKA-dependent signaling cascades (Gerfen et al., 1990; Kebabian &amp; Calne, 1979). Functionally, activation of this cell promotes selected motor actions by disinhibiting thalamic and midbrain motor centers (Mink, 1996; Cui et al., 2013)." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:36741471"

- [direct pathway medium spiny neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023026) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "Despite the direct and indirect circuits are often described not only as functionally opposing but also as anatomically segregated there are several anatomical and functional studies that have challenged this notion of pure segregation based on extensive collateral projections between pathways, dual-projection neurons, simultaneous co-activation during behavior."

#### Added

- [fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4072104) [contributor](http://purl.org/dc/terms/contributor) [0009-0000-8480-9277](https://orcid.org/0009-0000-8480-9277) 

- [fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4072104) [in_subset](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#inSubset) [human_subset](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/cl#human_subset) 

- [fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4072104) [in_subset](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#inSubset) [mouse_subset](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/cl#mouse_subset) 

- [fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4072104) [has narrow synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasNarrowSynonym) "meniscus fibrochondrocyte" 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:28939894" 

- [fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4072104) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A chondrocyte with hybrid fibroblastic-chondrogenic characteristics found in fibrocartilage, particularly in the avascular inner zone and transitional middle zone of the meniscus. In humans, fibrochondrocytes are marked by predominant expression of type I collagen (COL1A1) and fibril-associated collagens (COL3A1, COL6A1), while retaining type II collagen (COL2A1) expression and exhibiting lower SOX9 than hyaline chondrocytes. This molecular profile underlies the synthesis of abundant type I collagen essential for fibrocartilage matrix and reflects an intermediate phenotype between fibroblast and chondrocyte." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:31871141" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:34608249" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:28939894" 

- [fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4072104) [has_related_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasRelatedSynonym) "FC" 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:31871141" 

  - [has_synonym_type](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasSynonymType) [abbreviation](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/OMO_0003000) 

- [fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4072104) [has exact synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "fibrocartilage chondrocyte" 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:34608249" 

- [fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4072104) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "fibrochondrocyte" 

- [fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4072104) EquivalentTo [chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000138) and ([part of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000050) some [fibrocartilage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0001995))

- [fibrochondrocyte progenitor cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020021) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A mesenchymal progenitor cell located in fibrocartilaginous tissues, along the fibrochondrocytic differentiation pathway that co-expresses both fibrochondrocyte markers (COL1A1, COL3A1) and mesenchymal stem cell markers (MCAM/CD146, MYLK) in humans. This cell serves as a progenitor for mature fibrochondrocytes and other meniscal cell types, with differentiation regulated by TGF-&beta; signaling, focal adhesion, and extracellular matrix-receptor interaction pathways." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:31871141"

### homeostatic chondrocyte `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020020`

#### Added
- Class: [homeostatic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020020) 

- [homeostatic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020020) [creator](http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/creator) "GitHub Copilot" 

- [homeostatic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020020) [contributor](http://purl.org/dc/terms/contributor) [0009-0000-8480-9277](https://orcid.org/0009-0000-8480-9277) 

- [homeostatic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020020) [in_subset](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#inSubset) [human_subset](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/cl#human_subset) 

- [homeostatic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020020) [in_subset](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#inSubset) [mouse_subset](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/cl#mouse_subset) 

- [homeostatic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020020) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A chondrocyte identified in both healthy and osteoarthritic human articular cartilage, and in intervertebral disc tissue. In healthy articular cartilage, a homeostatic chondrocyte is characterised by the expression of TXNIP, IFITM3, GDF15, and TIMP1 (Wang et al., 2021), among other extracellular matrix and regulatory molecules. This cell maintains cartilage integrity by producing key ECM components and supporting baseline tissue homeostasis. In OA cartilage, this cell is enriched for genes related to cellular homeostasis modulation, including regulation of the cell cycle, development, and RNA metabolism (Ji et al., 2018)." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:34400611" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:37660146" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:30026257" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:34045450"

### hypertrophic chondrocyte `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000743`
#### Removed
- [hypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000743) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "Chondrocyte that is terminally differentiated, produces type X collagen, is large in size, and often associated with the replacement of cartilage by bone (endochondral ossification)." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "GO_REF:0000034" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:15951842" 

- [hypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000743) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "is hypertrophic pathological or normal? and can it be described using a pato term?" 

#### Added
- [hypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000743) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A chondrocyte that is part of the hypertrophic cartilage zone. This cell is significantly enlarged and characterised by high expression of type X collagen (COL10A1) in both humans and mice. It actively coordinates endochondral ossification by mineralising the extracellular matrix, attracting blood vessels via angiogenic signalling, and mediating the transition from cartilage to bone - often by transdifferentiating into an osteoblast rather than undergoing apoptosis." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "GO_REF:0000034" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:15951842" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:35179487" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:25321476" 

- [hypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000743) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "Despite historical descriptions as 'terminally differentiated,' hypertrophic chondrocytes survive and transdifferentiate into osteoblasts. Genetic lineage tracing shows that hypertrophic chondrocytes do not simply undergo apoptosis but cross the cartilage&ndash;bone boundary, dedifferentiate into skeletal stem/progenitor cells, and then redifferentiate into osteoblasts and osteocytes. Single-cell RNA-seq further indicates that these chondrocyte-derived SSPCs are a major source of trabecular osteoblasts and marrow adipocytes." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:35179487" 

- [hypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000743) EquivalentTo [chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000138) and ([part of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000050) some [hypertrophic cartilage zone](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0008187)) 

- [hypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000743) SubClassOf [bone cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0001035) 

- [hypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000743) SubClassOf [part of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000050) some [hypertrophic cartilage zone](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0008187) 

- [hypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000743) SubClassOf [capable of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002215) some [endochondral ossification](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/GO_0001958) 

- [hypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000743) SubClassOf [expresses](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002292) some [collagen alpha-1(X) chain](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/PR_000005693)

### indirect pathway medium spiny neuron `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023029`
#### Removed
- [indirect pathway medium spiny neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023029) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A medium spiny neuron that expresses dopamine type 2 receptors and projects to the external globus pallidus." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:34727523" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "WikipediaVersioned:Medium_spiny_neuron&amp;oldid=1109726850" 

#### Added
- [indirect pathway medium spiny neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023029) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "Despite the direct and indirect circuits are often described not only as functionally opposing but also as anatomically segregated there are several anatomical and functional studies that have challenged this notion of pure segregation based on extensive collateral projections between pathways, dual-projection neurons, simultaneous co-activation during behavior." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:26018615" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:29737578" 

- [indirect pathway medium spiny neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023029) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A GABAergic medium spiny neuron located in the striatum that gives rise to the indirect basal ganglia pathway. It projects to the GPe, where its axon typically ramifies in two regions but does not extend beyond this nucleus (Gerfen et al., 2022). It selectively expresses the D2 dopamine receptor (DRD2), which couples to inhibitory G-proteins (Gi/o) to decrease cAMP and suppress PKA-mediated signaling (Gerfen et al., 2022). Morphologically, this cell displays fewer and shorter dendrites than the MSN-D1 and receives fewer glutamatergic inputs, yet it exhibits significantly higher intrinsic excitability (Gertler et al., 2022). Functionally, activation of this cell suppresses competing or alternative motor actions by inhibiting GPe neurons, leading through STN and other GPe circuits to increased GPi/SNr output and stronger inhibition of thalamic and brainstem targets (Mink, 1996; Tecuapetla et al., 2016)." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:36741471" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:34727523" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:9004351" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:27453468" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "WikipediaVersioned:Medium_spiny_neuron&amp;oldid=1109726850"

- [osteochondral skeletal stem cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020016) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A tissue-specific stem cell with long-term self-renewal capacity that is restricted to generating bone, cartilage, and stromal cell lineages. This cell is primarily located in the growth plate (resting zone), periosteum, and subchondral bone regions, and is marked by high clonogenicity and robust multipotent differentiation potential in both osteogenic and chondrogenic lineages. Distinctively, ocSSC lacks adipogenic capacity, distinguishing it from other mesenchymal stem cell populations." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "doi:10.1101/2023.12.07.570646"

### prehypertrophic chondrocyte `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020022`

#### Added
- Class: [prehypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020022) 

- [prehypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020022) [contributor](http://purl.org/dc/terms/contributor) [0009-0000-8480-9277](https://orcid.org/0009-0000-8480-9277) 

- [prehypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020022) [in_subset](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#inSubset) [human_subset](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/cl#human_subset) 

- [prehypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020022) [in_subset](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#inSubset) [mouse_subset](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/cl#mouse_subset) 

- [prehypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020022) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A post-proliferative chondrocyte in the prehypertrophic zone of the cartilage tissue, located between the proliferative and hypertrophic zones. This cell is characterised by increased cell volume and expression of Indian Hedgehog (Ihh), PTH1R, and Runx2/3 in both humans and mice (Hallett et al., 2021). It coordinates the PTHrP-Ihh feedback loop that regulates chondrocyte differentiation and functions as a signalling hub for communication between proliferative chondrocytes, hypertrophic chondrocytes, and periosteal osteoblasts (Hallett et al., 2021)." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:31871141" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:29985449" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:34137454" 

- [prehypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020022) [has_related_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasRelatedSynonym) "preHTC" 
  - [has_synonym_type](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasSynonymType) [abbreviation](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/OMO_0003000) 

- [prehypertrophic chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020022) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "prehypertrophic chondrocyte"

- [proliferative fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020018) [creator](http://purl.org/dc/terms/creator) "GitHub Copilot" 

- [proliferative fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020018) [date](http://purl.org/dc/terms/date) "2025-11-27T12:48:39Z"^^[dateTime](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#dateTime) 

- [proliferative fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020018) [in_subset](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#inSubset) [human_subset](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/cl#human_subset) 

- [proliferative fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020018) [in_subset](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#inSubset) [mouse_subset](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/cl#mouse_subset) 

- [proliferative fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020018) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A fibrochondrocyte located in fibrocartilage that exhibits active proliferation capacity and is in S phase of the cell cycle. It functions as a progenitor cell positioned at the root of developmental trajectories alongside fibrochondrocyte progenitors (FCP), with the capacity to diverge toward one of two developmental fates: (1) fibrochondrocytes and prehypertrophic chondrocytes, or (2) regulatory chondrocytes and prehypertrophic chondrocytes. It is characterised by co-expression of COL1A1, the growth factors FGF7 and CTGF, and the cell-cycle genes STMN1, KIAA0101, and MCM3 in humans. During early progenitor differentiation, FGF7 and COL1A1 expression increases and then declines as the cell commits to terminal fates." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:31871141" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:39759119" 

- [proliferative fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020018) [has_related_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasRelatedSynonym) "ProFC" 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:31871141" 

  - [has_synonym_type](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasSynonymType) [abbreviation](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/OMO_0003000) 

- [proliferative fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020018) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "Lineage relationships are inferred from single-cell RNA-seq trajectories and validated through experimental approaches, including FACS isolation, functional differentiation assays, and in vivo developmental gene expression analysis." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:31871141" 

- [proliferative fibrochondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020018) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "proliferative fibrochondrocyte"

### regulatory chondrocyte `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020019`

#### Added
- Class: [regulatory chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020019) 

- [regulatory chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020019) [creator](http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/creator) "GitHub Copilot" 

- [regulatory chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020019) [contributor](http://purl.org/dc/terms/contributor) [0009-0000-8480-9277](https://orcid.org/0009-0000-8480-9277) 

- [regulatory chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020019) [in_subset](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#inSubset) [human_subset](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/cl#human_subset) 

- [regulatory chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020019) [in_subset](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#inSubset) [mouse_subset](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/cl#mouse_subset) 

- [regulatory chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020019) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A chondrocyte located mainly in the superficial zone of articular cartilage. In healthy human cartilage, regulatory chondrocytes are characterized by expression of EIF5A, PGK1, ANXA1, and TUBA1A. During osteoarthritis, a distinct subpopulation expands, marked by high expression of CHI3L1, CHI3L2, CRTAC1, and AEBP1, with enrichment for signaling pathway regulation (including Toll-like receptor, mTOR, and TGF-beta signaling) and antigen-processing gene expression, with a small proportion expressing MHC class II genes, suggesting potential immune cell-like regulatory functions during osteoarthritis progression." 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:37660146" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:30026257" 

  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:34045450" 

- [regulatory chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020019) [has_related_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasRelatedSynonym) "RegC" 
  - [has cross-reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref) "PMID:37660146" 

- [regulatory chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020019) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "regulatory chondrocyte" 

- [regulatory chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0020019) SubClassOf [chondrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000138)
